# <a name="dimensions-and-measurements-available-in-call-quality-dashboard-cqd"></a><span data-ttu-id="9485f-103">CQD 呼叫质量仪表板中提供的维度 (度量) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-103">Dimensions and measurements available in Call Quality Dashboard (CQD)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9485f-104">使用 CQD (Microsoft Teams) Skype for Business Online 的 CQD 仪表板，你可以更好地了解使用这些服务进行呼叫的呼叫质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-104">The Call Quality Dashboard (CQD) for Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business Online allows you to better understand call quality of calls made with these services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9485f-105">本主题提供有关通过 CQD 可见的维度和度量的详细信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-105">This topic provides detailed information about the dimensions and measurements visible through CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9485f-106">若要详细了解 CQD，请参阅"[使用 CQD 管理 Microsoft Teams 中的通话和会议质量"。](quality-of-experience-review-guide.md)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-106">To learn more about CQD, see [Use CQD to manage call and meeting quality in Microsoft Teams](quality-of-experience-review-guide.md).</span></span>

## <a name="first-and-second-endpoint-classification"></a><span data-ttu-id="9485f-107">第一和第二终结点分类</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-107">First and Second endpoint classification</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9485f-108">CQD 中的许多维度和度量都标记为第一个或第二个。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-108">Many of the dimensions and measurements in CQD are labeled as first or second.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9485f-109">以下逻辑用于确定将流或通话中涉及的哪些终结点标为第一。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-109">The following logic determines which endpoint involved in the stream or call is labeled as first:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="9485f-110">当服务器 (流或调用时，) AV MCU、中介服务器等服务器终结点视为"先"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-110">A Server endpoint (AV MCU, Mediation Server, and so on) is considered First when a Server is involved in the stream or call.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="9485f-111">除非流在两个服务器终结点之间，否则客户端终结点被视为第二终结点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-111">A Client endpoint is considered Second unless the stream is between two Server endpoints.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="9485f-112">如果两个终结点的类型相同，则首先根据用户代理类别的内部顺序设置第一个和第二个终结点，以确保顺序一致。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-112">If both endpoints are the same type, first vs. second is set based on internal ordering of the user agent category to ensure that the ordering is consistent.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9485f-113">例如，此处每行表示流中涉及的一对用户代理：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-113">For example, here each row represents a pair of User Agents involved in a stream:</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-114">呼叫方的用户代理类别</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-114">User Agent Category of Caller</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-115">被叫方的用户代理类别</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-115">User Agent Category of Callee</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-116">First Endpoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-116">First Endpoint</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-117">Second Endpoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-117">Second Endpoint</span></span>|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-118">First Is Caller</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-118">First Is Caller</span></span>
|:--- |:--- |:--- |:--- |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-119">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-119">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-120">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-120">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-121">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-121">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-122">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-122">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-123">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-123">TRUE</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-124">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-124">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-125">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-125">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-126">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-126">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-127">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-127">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-128">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-128">FALSE</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-129">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-129">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-130">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-130">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-131">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-131">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-132">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-132">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-133">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-133">FALSE</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-134">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-134">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-135">中介服务器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-135">Mediation Server</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-136">中介服务器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-136">Mediation Server</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-137">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-137">AV-MCU</span></span> ||
|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-138">中介服务器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-138">Mediation Server</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-139">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-139">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-140">中介服务器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-140">Mediation Server</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-141">AV-MCU</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-141">AV-MCU</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-142">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-142">TRUE</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-143">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-143">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-144">OC 电话（Skype for Business IP 电话）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-144">OC Phone (Skype for Business IP Phone)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-145">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-145">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-146">OC 电话（Skype for Business IP 电话）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-146">OC Phone (Skype for Business IP Phone)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-147">是</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-147">TRUE</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-148">OC 电话（Skype for Business IP 电话）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-148">OC Phone (Skype for Business IP Phone)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-149">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-149">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-150">OC（Skype for Business 客户端）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-150">OC (Skype for Business client)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-151">OC 电话（Skype for Business IP 电话）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-151">OC Phone (Skype for Business IP Phone)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-152">否</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-152">FALSE</span></span> |

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="9485f-p103">[!注释] 第一和第二分类与终结点是呼叫方还是被叫方无关。"第一是呼叫方"维度可以用来帮助确定哪个终结点是呼叫方或被叫方。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-p103">That First and Second classification is separate from which endpoint is the caller or callee. The First Is Caller dimension can be used to help identify which endpoint was the caller or callee.</span></span>

## <a name="dimensions"></a><span data-ttu-id="9485f-155">维度</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-155">Dimensions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9485f-156">维度信息部分基于上传到 CQD 门户的数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-156">Dimensions information is based in part on data uploaded to the CQD portal.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9485f-157">许多维度值也可以用作筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-157">Many Dimension values can also be used as filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9485f-158">下表列出了 CQD 中当前可用的维度，按查询编辑器中列出的顺序创建报表或编辑以前定义的报表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-158">The following table lists the dimensions currently available in CQD, in the order listed in the Query Editor used to create reports or edit previously defined reports.</span></span>

### <a name="notes-on-dimension-data-typeunits"></a><span data-ttu-id="9485f-2497">维度值/单位数据类型说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2497">Notes on dimension data type/units</span></span>

#### <a name="boolean"></a><span data-ttu-id="9485f-2498">Boolean</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2498">Boolean</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2499">布尔值始终为 True 或 False。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2499">Boolean values are always either True or False.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9485f-2500">在某些情况下，True 也可以表示为 1，False 可以表示为 0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2500">In some cases, True can also be represented as 1 and False can be represented as 0.</span></span>

#### <a name="range"></a><span data-ttu-id="9485f-2501">范围</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2501">Range</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2502">按范围或分组表示的维度值使用以下格式显示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2502">Dimensions that are provided as range or group of values are shown using the following format:</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="9485f-2503">_\<sort order string\> [\<lower bound inclusive\> - \<upper bound exclusive\>_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2503">_\<sort order string\> [\<lower bound inclusive\> - \<upper bound exclusive\>_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2504">例如，持续时间（分钟）维度表示以分钟为单位的通话持续时间，报告的值以取值范围的形式表示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2504">For example, the Duration (Minutes) dimension represents the call duration in seconds with the value reported as a range of values.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2505">Duration (Minutes)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2505">Duration (Minutes)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2506">解释方法</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2506">How to interpret</span></span> |
|:--- |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2507">062: [0 - 0)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2507">062: [0 - 0)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2508">流持续时间 = 0 分钟</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2508">Stream duration = 0 minutes</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2509">064: [1 - 2)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2509">064: [1 - 2)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2510">1 分钟 < = 流持续时间 < 2 分钟</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2510">1 minute < = stream duration < 2 minutes</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2511">065: [2 - 3)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2511">065: [2 - 3)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2512">2 分钟 < = 流持续时间 < 3 分钟</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2512">2 minutes < = stream duration < 3 minutes</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2513">066：[3-4) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2513">066: [3–4)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2514">3 分钟 < = 流持续时间 < 4 分钟</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2514">3 minutes < = stream duration < 4 minutes</span></span> |
|  | |

<span data-ttu-id="9485f-p315">The \<sort order string> is used to control the sort order when presenting the data and can be used for filtering. For example, a filter on Duration (Minutes) < "065", would show streams with duration less than 2 minutes (The leading '0' is needed for the filter to work as expected).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-p315">The \<sort order string> is used to control the sort order when presenting the data and can be used for filtering. For example, a filter on Duration (Minutes) < "065", would show streams with duration less than 2 minutes (The leading '0' is needed for the filter to work as expected).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="9485f-2517">[!注释] 排序字符串的实际值并不重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2517">The actual value of the sort order string isn't significant.</span></span>

#### <a name="enumeration-strings"></a><span data-ttu-id="9485f-2518">枚举字符串</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2518">Enumeration strings</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2519">CQD 使用的字符串通常派生自数据文件，这些字符串几乎可以是允许长度内的任意字符组合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2519">Strings used by CQD are often derived from data files, and these can be nearly any combination of character within the allowed length.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9485f-2520">某些维度看起来像字符串，但由于它们只能是预定义值的简短列表之一，因此它们是枚举而不是真正的字符串。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2520">Some dimensions look like strings, but since they can only be one of a short list of predefined values, they are enumerations and not true strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9485f-2521">某些枚举字符串也用于成对。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2521">Some enumerations strings are also used in pairs.</span></span>

#### <a name="enumeration-pair"></a><span data-ttu-id="9485f-2522">枚举对</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2522">Enumeration pair</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2523">按枚举对表示的维度使用以下格式显示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2523">Dimensions that are provided as an enumeration pair are shown using the following format:</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="9485f-2524">_\<enumeration value from one end point\> : \<enumeration value from the other endpoint\>_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2524">_\<enumeration value from one end point\> : \<enumeration value from the other endpoint\>_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2525">枚举值的顺序一致，但此顺序不反映第一或第二终结点的顺序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2525">The ordering of the enumeration values is consistent but doesn't reflect ordering of the first or second endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2526">例如，网络连接详情对显示两个终结点的网络连接详情值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2526">For example, the Network Connection Detail Pair shows the Network Connection Detail values for the two endpoints:</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2527">Network Connection Detail Pair</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2527">Network Connection Detail Pair</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2528">解释方法</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2528">How to interpret</span></span> |
|:--- |:--- |
|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2529">有线 : 有线</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2529">Wired : Wired</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2530">第一和第二终结点均使用有线以太网连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2530">First and second endpoints both used wired ethernet connections.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2531">有线 : wifi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2531">Wired : wifi</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2532">第一个终结点使用有线以太网连接且第二个终结点使用 Wi-Fi 连接，或第二个终结点使用有线以太网连接且第一个终结点使用 Wi-Fi 连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2532">First endpoint used wired ethernet connection and second endpoint used Wi-Fi connection, or the second endpoint used wired ethernet connection and first endpoint used Wi-Fi connection.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2533">: wifi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2533">: wifi</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2534">第一个终结点使用 WiFi 连接且第二个终结点使用的网络连接未知，或第二个终结点使用 WiFi 连接且第一个终结点使用的网络连接未知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2534">First endpoint used a WiFi connection and the network connection used by the second endpoint is unknown, or the second endpoint used a WiFi connection and the network connection used by the first endpoint is unknown.</span></span> |
| | |

#### <a name="blank-values"></a><span data-ttu-id="9485f-2535">空值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2535">Blank values</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2536">上表列出了维度可能出现空值的原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2536">The table above lists possible reasons why a dimension may be blank.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9485f-2537">如果 QoE 记录可用维度为 false，则许多维度和度量将为空。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2537">Many dimensions and measurements will be blank if the QoE Record Available dimension is false.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9485f-2538">这通常出现在通话未能成功建立的情况下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2538">This typically occurs when the call wasn't successfully established.</span></span>

## <a name="measurements"></a><span data-ttu-id="9485f-2539">度量</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2539">Measurements</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2540">许多度量值也可以用作筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2540">Many Measurement values can also be used as filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9485f-2541">下表列出了 CQD 中当前可用的度量，按查询编辑器中列出的顺序显示</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2541">The following table lists the measurements currently available in CQD, shown in the order listed in the Query Editor</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2542">衡量指标名称</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2542">Measure Name</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2543">单位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2543">Units</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2544">说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2544">Description</span></span> |
|:--- |:--- |:--- |

| <span data-ttu-id="9485f-2548">CDR 可用流计数总计</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2548">Total CDR Available Stream Count</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="9485f-2549">流的数量</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2549">Number of streams</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2550">提供可靠性/诊断信息的媒体流的数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2550">Number of media streams with reliability/diagnostics information available.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9485f-2551">在 [Skype for Business Server (CDR) 通话详细信息](https://docs.microsoft.com/skypeforbusiness/manage/health-and-monitoring/call-detail-recording-cdr)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2551">See [Call detail recording (CDR) in Skype for Business Server](https://docs.microsoft.com/skypeforbusiness/manage/health-and-monitoring/call-detail-recording-cdr)</span></span> |

|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2573">Total Answer Seizure Ratio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2573">Total Answer Seizure Ratio</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2574">比率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2574">Ratio</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2575">持续时间低于 5 秒钟的通话占通话总数的比率。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2575">Ratio of calls with duration less than 5 seconds over the total number of calls.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2576">Total Short Call Percentage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2576">Total Short Call Percentage</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2577">百分比</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2577">Percentage</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2578">总通话时间小于 1 分钟的百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2578">Percentage of total calls less than 1 minute long.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2579">Total Media Failure Percentage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2579">Total Media Failure Percentage</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2580">百分比</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2580">Percentage</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2581">媒体路径未能建立或未正常终止的所有流的百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2581">Percentage of all streams where either media path could not be established or did not terminate normally.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2582">总音频流持续时间 (分钟) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2582">Total Audio Stream Duration (Minutes)</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2583">分钟数</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2583">Minutes</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2584">所选时间范围内的总音频流持续时间（以分钟数表示）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2584">Total audio stream duration in minutes in the selected time range.</span></span> |
|<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2585">Media Failed Due To Firewall DPI Stream Count</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2585">Media Failed Due To Firewall DPI Stream Count</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2586">流的数量</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2586">Number of streams</span></span> |<span data-ttu-id="9485f-2587">由于深度包检测不允许 Skype for Business 流量导致网络设备阻止访问进而未能建立的流的数量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2587">Number of streams that failed to be established due to network equipment blocking access due to deep packet inspection not allowing Skype for Business traffic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9485f-2588">这些故障通常表示代理、防火墙或其他网络安全设备未正确配置为访问 Microsoft 365 或 Office 365 中的 Skype for Business 使用的 IP 地址和端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-2588">These failures typically indicate a proxy, firewall or other network security device is not correctly configured to access the IP address and ports used by Skype for Business in Microsoft 365 or Office 365.</span></span> |

### <a name="notes-on-measurements"></a><span data-ttu-id="9485f-3164">度量说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-3164">Notes on measurements</span></span>

#### <a name="accuracy-limitations"></a><span data-ttu-id="9485f-3165">准确性限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-3165">Accuracy limitations</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="9485f-3166">某些用户和调用计数度量依赖于对数据集执行不同的 countif 操作来计算计数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-3166">Certain user and call count measurements rely on performing a distinct countif operation on the data set to compute the count.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9485f-3167">根据执行该操作的行数，不同 countif 操作目前存在最多 0.2% 的固有错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-3167">There is currently an up to 0.2% error inherent with the distinct countif operation depending on the number of rows the operation is performed on.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9485f-3168">对于最准确的卷，应该使用流计数度量值，因为它们不依赖于此不同的 countif 操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-3168">For the most accurate volume, you should use stream count measures since they do not rely on this distinct countif operation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9485f-3169">用于减少数据量的筛选可以减少错误，但可能无法消除不同调用和用户计数中的此错误源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-3169">Filtering to reduce the data volume may reduce the error but may not eliminate this source of error in distinct call and user counts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9485f-3170">有关此限制详细信息，可在此处找到 [dcount 聚合函数](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/data-explorer/kusto/query/dcount-aggfunction)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-3170">More information about this limitation can be found here [dcount aggregate function](https://docs.microsoft.com/azure/data-explorer/kusto/query/dcount-aggfunction).</span></span>

## <a name="filters"></a><span data-ttu-id="9485f-3171">筛选器</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-3171">Filters</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="9485f-3172">许多维度和度量值也可以用作筛选器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-3172">Many Dimension and Measurement values can also be used as filters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="9485f-3173">可以使用查询中的筛选器来消除信息，方法与选择维度或度量以在查询中添加或包含信息的方式相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="9485f-3173">You can use filters in your query to eliminate information in the same way you'd select a Dimension or Measurement to add or include information in the query.</span></span>
